 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Announcement: </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The
Goldman Sachs Trust (&#147;GST&#148;) and Goldman Sachs Variable Insurance Trust (&#147;VIT&#148;) will be holding a special meeting on January&nbsp;23, 2020 (the &#147;Special Meeting&#148;), requesting shareholders to consider and vote on one or
more fund proposals (the &#147;Proposals&#148;), as outlined below. Shareholders and variable contract owners are not required to attend the Special Meeting and it is expected that most shareholders and variable contract owners will vote their
shares by proxy. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>How will this impact clients? </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Between the record date and Special Meeting date, shareholders may receive various communications from Goldman Sachs and/or their financial intermediary to
solicit their vote on the Proposals. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Timeline: </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">I can resend the proxy materials to you, or I can review the proposals with you and record your vote immediately by phone. &lt;Pause for response&gt; </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Your Board recommends that you vote <B>&#147;FOR&#148;</B> the proposals. Would you like to vote along with the recommendations of the Board for all your

YOUR VOTE BY JANUARY&nbsp;22, 2020 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Recently, we sent you proxy material regarding a shareholder meeting scheduled for January&nbsp;23, 2020. Our records
indicate that we have not received your voting instructions. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">We urge you to vote as soon as possible in order to allow the Funds to obtain a sufficient
number of votes to hold the meeting as scheduled. <B>Join your fellow holders and vote today!</B> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">If you have any questions or would like
to vote, please call the number listed below: </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-800-574-5796</FONT></FONT></FONT> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Your vote is important no matter the size of the shares you own. Please vote promptly so
your vote can be received by the January&nbsp;23, 2020 meeting of shareholders. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>The Fund has made it very easy for you to vote.
Choose one of the following methods: </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Vote live with a Proxy Specialist</U></B> &#150; You may cast your vote live with a
proxy specialist, quickly and easily, and have proxy related questions answered, by calling toll free:
<B><U><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">1-800-574-5796.</FONT></FONT></FONT></U></B> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Vote via the Internet</U> </B>&#150; You may cast your vote using the Internet by logging onto the Internet address located on your proxy
ballot(s) and following the instructions on the website. <U><B>www.proxyvote.com</B></U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Vote by Touch-Tone Phone</U></B> &#150; You
may cast your vote by telephone by calling the toll-free number found on the proxy ballot(s) that you received. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; margin-left:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><U>Vote by
Mail</U></B><B> &#150; </B>You may cast your vote by signing, dating and mailing your proxy ballot(s) in the postage prepaid return envelope that was previously provided to you. </P>
